        (function() {
            var ep;
            var loginState;
            try {
                window.localStorage && (ep = JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem('dl_ep') || "false"));
                window.localStorage && (loginState = JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem('dl_loginState')) || undefined);
            } catch (e) {
                console.error(e);
            }

            
            // read release groups cookie
            var releaseGroups = [];
            try {
                if (document.cookie) {
                    var allCookies = document.cookie.split('; ');
                    var releaseGroupsCookie = '';

                    for (i = 0; i < allCookies.length; i++) {
                        var cookiePair = allCookies[i].split('=');
                        if ('releaseGroups' === cookiePair[0].trim()) {
                            releaseGroupsCookie = cookiePair[1];
                        }
                    }

                    if (releaseGroupsCookie) {
                        // structure: id.name.variant.breakout_id.name.variant.breakout ...
                        var groups = releaseGroupsCookie.split('_');

                        for (i = 0; i < groups.length; i++) {
                            var group = groups[i].split('.');

                            if (group.length === 4) {
                                releaseGroups.push({
                                    id: parseInt(group[0], 10) || 0,
                                    name: group[1],
                                    variant: parseInt(group[2], 10) || 0,
                                    breakout: parseInt(group[3], 10) || 0
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.error(e);
            }

            // read recommendation cookie
            var userRecommendations = [];
            try {
                if (document.cookie) {
                    var allCookies = document.cookie.split('; ');
                    var userRecommendationsCookie = '';

                    for (i = 0; i < allCookies.length; i++) {
                        var cookiePair = allCookies[i].split('=');
                        if ('userRecommendations' === cookiePair[0].trim()) {
                            userRecommendationsCookie = cookiePair[1];
                        }
                    }

                    if (userRecommendationsCookie) {
                        // structure: name.variant_name.variant ...
                        var recommendations = userRecommendationsCookie.split('_');

                        for (i = 0; i < recommendations.length; i++) {
                            var recommendation = recommendations[i].split('.');

                            if (recommendation.length === 2) {
                                userRecommendations.push({
                                    name: recommendation[0],
                                    variant: parseInt(recommendation[1], 10) || 0
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.error(e);
            }

            window.dl_pageState = {
                v: '20180814',
                il: 'ja',
                dataUseProhibited: !!(document.cookie || "").match(/(^| )data-use-prohibited=[^;]+/)
                ,
				logoutTarget: '/translator',
				relCanonical: '/translator',
				dapPageId: '110',
				dapEndpointV2: 'https://s.deepl.com/web/statistics',
				dapReleaseGroups: 'https://s.deepl.com/web/release-groups',
				supportUrl: 'https://support.deepl.com',
				secureCookie: '1',
				featureFlags: ['app_docTrans_uploadBtn_2020_07_mac','app_docTrans_uploadBtn_2020_07_win','banner_ad_202008','canadaUSProRelease_2020_04','charCount_apps_ad','clearance','docTrans_backend_v2','docTrans_free_limit_2021_01','freeApi_2021_02','langDetection_2020_09','ltSEO_2020_10','notifications_react_2020_10','pro_brands_2020_08','pro_footer_2020_08','sso','support_zendesk_guide_2021_03','translatorTrackingApp_2020-08','translatorTracking_2020-07','upgradeFlows_2020_09','newEULangsProDocTrans_2020_12','sentry','newInterfaceLang_SV_2021_06','newInterfaceLang_CS_2021_12','pro_pdf_2022_01','free_pdf_2022_01',]
            };

            if (loginState && loginState.accountId) {
                dl_pageState.loginState = loginState;
                document.documentElement.classList.add('dl_user_logged_in');
            } else if (ep) {
                dl_pageState.ep = ep
                document.documentElement.classList.add('dl_ep');
            }
            if (ep || (loginState && loginState.accountId)) {
                dl_pageState.pro = true;
                document.documentElement.classList.add('dl_pro');
            }

    <script>
    (function(){
        const loc = ((decodeURIComponent(""+location.pathname).match(/^.*?\/translator.*?\/(.*)($|\?)|/)||[])[1] || "");
        const parts = loc.split("/");
        if (parts.length < 3)
            return;
        let updateMetaNodes = false, mode = parts[0];
        if (mode==='l' || mode==='q'){  parts.shift(); } else { mode = 'q'; }
        let initialState, newPageId;
        const a = parts.map(function(s){ return s.replace(/\+/g, " ")}), revert = [];
        if (mode==='q'){
            const s = parts.join("/");
            let v = 0x811c9dc5;
            for(let i = s.length - 1; i>=0; --i ){v ^= s.charCodeAt(i); v += (v << 1) + (v << 4) + (v << 7) + (v << 8) + (v << 24);}
            const checked = (v >>> 0).toString(16).match(/73536$/);
            revert.push(function(){window.history.replaceState(null, "", (location.href.match(/^.*?translator/g)||[])[0]);});
            initialState = { sourceLangcode:a[0], sourceText:a[1], targetLangcode:a[2], revert: revert, };
            if (checked){
                initialState.checked = true;
                initialState.sourceChains = [[a[1]]];
                initialState.targetChains = [[a[3]]];
                updateMetaNodes = true;
                const originalTitle = document.title;
                document.title = a[1] + " (" + a[0] + ") - " + originalTitle;
                revert.push(function(){ document.title = originalTitle });
                newPageId = 1200;
            }
        } else if (mode==='l'){
            initialState = { sourceLangcode:a[0], targetLangcode:a[1], revert: revert, checked: true };
            updateMetaNodes = true;
            const originalTitle = document.title;
            document.title = originalTitle + " - (" + a[0] + ")";
            revert.push(function(){ document.title = originalTitle });
            newPageId = 1201;
        }
        if (updateMetaNodes){
            const linkNodes = document.querySelectorAll("link[rel=alternate], link[rel=canonical]");
            for (let i=0; i<linkNodes.length; ++i){
                const n = linkNodes[i], originalHref = n.getAttribute('href') || "";
                n.setAttribute('href', originalHref.replace('translator', 'translator/' + loc));
                revert.push(function(){n.setAttribute('href', originalHref)});
            }
            const metaNodes = document.querySelectorAll("meta[property^=og]");
            for (let i=0; i<metaNodes.length; ++i){
                const n = metaNodes[i];
                n.parentElement.removeChild(n);
            }
        }
        if (newPageId && window.dl_pageState){
            const originalDapPageId = window.dl_pageState.dapPageId;
            window.dl_pageState.dapPageId = newPageId;
            revert.push(function(){
                if (window.store && window.store.getState().pageState) {
                    var payload = Object.assign({}, window.dl_pageState);
                    payload.dapPageId = originalDapPageId;
                    window.store.dispatch({
                        type: 'pagestate/change',
                        payload: payload
                    });
                } else {
                    window.dl_pageState.dapPageId = originalDapPageId;
                }
            });
        }

        window._initialTranslatorState = initialState;
    })();

    })()

    <script>
        if (!(!!window.MSInputMethodContext && !!document.documentMode)) {
            document.querySelector('.ie11Modal_backdrop').remove();
        } else {
            var closeModal = function() {
                var child =  document.querySelector('.ie11Modal_backdrop');
                child.parentNode.removeChild(child);

                document.removeEventListener('keyup', closeOnEscapeListener);
            }

            var closeOnEscapeListener = function(event) {
                if (event.keyCode === 27) {
                    closeModal();
                }
            }

            document.addEventListener('keyup', closeOnEscapeListener);
        }
    </script>

    <script>
    dl_documentReady(function() {
        M.requireAsync(['WebTranslator_proAd', 'WebTranslator_appPopup', 'LMT_InitializedWebTranslatorInstance', 'dlPageState', 'DeviceProps'], function(WebTranslator_proAd, WebTranslator_appPopup, webTranslator, dlPageState, DeviceProps) {
            if (DeviceProps.isMobilePhone) {
                // Init status
                if (!webTranslator.sourceIsEmpty()) {
                    WebTranslator_proAd.init();
                }
                // Listener
                webTranslator.sourceIsEmpty.onValueChanged.push(function (isSourceEmpty) {
                    if (!isSourceEmpty) {
                        WebTranslator_proAd.init();
                        return 'REMOVE';
                    }
                });
            } else {
                WebTranslator_proAd.init();
                WebTranslator_appPopup.init();
            }
        });
    });
    </script>

    <script>
        M.define('LMT_InitializedWebTranslatorInstance', ['Translator_web', 'LMT_WebTranslator_Instance', '$', 'dlPageState', 'dlClientState', 'dlPrivacy', 'DeviceProps', 'queryVars', 'H2'],
                function(Translator_web , webTranslator, $, dlPageState, dlClientState, dlPrivacy, DeviceProps, queryVars, H2){
            $("html").addClass("page_loaded");
            Translator_web.initTranslator(webTranslator);
            
            // Wait for glossary to be loaded (removeReason is in the glossary module) if it should be turned on
            if (!DeviceProps.isMobilePhone) {
                webTranslator.features.get('/translator/core/updateSourceSentences').addReasonToDelayUpdates("waitingForGlossary");
            }

            if (!dlPageState.pro) {
                M.requireAsync('WebTranslator_quotes', function(WebTranslator_quotes){
                    WebTranslator_quotes.init();
                });
            }

            M.requireAsync('WebTranslator_iosAppBanner', function(WebTranslator_iosAppBanner) {
                WebTranslator_iosAppBanner.init()
            })

            
            return webTranslator;
        });
    </script>
